     <div class="entry-content content"> 
      <div id="cs-content" class="cs-content">
       <div id="x-section-1" class="x-section bg-image" style="margin:0;padding:45px 0;background-image:url(https://perthweb.com.au/wp-content/uploads/2016/12/internal_headers3.jpg);background-color:transparent" data-x-element="section" data-x-params="{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;image&quot;,&quot;parallax&quot;:false}">
        <div class="x-container max width" style="margin: 0px auto;padding: 0px;">
         <div class="x-column x-sm cs-ta-center x-1-1" style="padding: 0px;">
          <img class="x-img x-img-none" src="https://perthweb.com.au/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/about-us-header.png" data-pagespeed-url-hash="242470118" onload="pagespeed.CriticalImages.checkImageForCriticality(this);">
          <!--The preceding resource was not rewritten because its domain (perthweb.com.au) is not authorized-->
          <h2 class="h-custom-headline h1" style="color: hsl(0, 0%, 100%);margin:15px 0;"><span>E-Commerce Solutions</span></h2>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
       <!--Flattening failed: Cannot rewrite https://perthweb.com.au/wp-content/uploads/2016/12/internal_headers3.jpg as it is on an unauthorized domain-->
       <div id="x-section-2" class="x-section" style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px 0px 45px; background-color: hsl(0, 0%, 100%);">
        <div class="x-container max width" style="margin: 0px auto;padding: 0px; background-color:hsla(0, 0%, 100%, 0);">
         <div class="x-column x-sm cs-ta-left x-1-1" style="padding: 0px;">
          <h1 class="h-custom-headline h1"><span>WOOCOMMERCE SHOPPING CART PACKAGE</span></h1>
          <div class="x-text">
           <p>This solution from PerthWeb provides businesses with a <strong>cost effective shopping cart that allows them to sell products online and easily update their own products via a password protected administration area</strong> on the web site. The solution can support 1000s of products and be extended in many ways including integration with accounting software. This solution is usually sold as a <strong>complete package including a web site and shopping cart from $4999 including GST</strong>, but it can also be <strong>added to an existing web WordPress web site from $2499 inclusive of GST</strong>. For clients with a smaller number of products we also offer our <a href="/shopping-cart-simple">Woocommerce Simple Shopping Cart</a> from $999 including GST.</p> 
           <p>See <a href="hhttps://www.homechef.com.au/">www.homechef.com.au</a>, <a href="http://www.hampersbydesign.com.au," target="_blank">www.hampersbydesign.com.au,</a> <a href="https://www.sensorykidsoutlet.com.au/">www.sensorykidsoutlet.com.au</a>, <a href="http://www.elitegymhire.com.au" target="_blank">www.elitegymhire.com.au</a> and <a href="http://www.aqualyte.com.au">www.aqualyte.com.au</a></p> 
          </div>
          <h3 class="h-custom-headline h3"><span>Shopping cart PACKAGE features:</span></h3>
          <div class="x-text">
           <ul> 
            <li>Utilises the popular WordPress Content Management System &amp; Woocommerce Shopping Cart solution, and includes documentation &amp; hands on training</li> 
            <li>Includes a high impact responsive (mobile friendly) web site design including up to 15 pages of general (non-product) content, stock photography, and a contact form for general web site queries</li> 
            <li>Supports the display of 1000s of products, which may be navigated by category or via key word search, and purchased online through PayPal or other payment solutions</li> 
            <li>An administration system which allows you to manage general web page content, add/edit/delete categories and products, view client &amp; order details, manage shipping rules, &amp; much more</li> 
            <li>Includes Google Analytics with goal tracking to monitor web site performance &amp; visitor behaviour to help ensure the best results from your web site</li>
